                   President of the World Peace Unification Family Association, Hwang Seonjo

1)
The World God Desires
Today, among those present here, please raise your hand if you are seeing me for the first time. Please lower your hands. After speaking a lot over the past few days, my throat is a bit hoarse. So please listen carefully. The title I want to share with you today is "The World God Desires." Let's talk about what kind of world God desires.

The current world lacks nations, ethnicities, families, and individuals that God desires. 
In this world we live in, there are many countries. Among those countries, there are nations formed by numerous ethnicities. Many nations have many ethnic groups living in them, and among those ethnic groups, there are countless families and individuals. Within this world, the question arises: is there a nation that God can truly love? This is an important question for us believers who are on the path of restoration, in other words, for those of us who are trying to fulfill God's will.

When we consider whether a country like the United States, which represents advanced nations, is a nation that God loves, it becomes a significant issue. If God does not love the United States, then what nation would He love? From this perspective, as you know, we can see that the society known as the United States is unlikely to become a progressive society in the future. It has come to represent hope for democratic nations around the world, but it is gradually moving away from that position. Furthermore, if we consider whether the once-great United States, which led the world, can maintain that position in the future, we see signs in various fields that it may not be able to.

Moreover, it is concerning that the youth issue has emerged as a serious social problem that could determine the fate of the nation. I have had ample opportunities to meet with various influential figures in the United States, and it is clear that the young people of that country should be the foundation that supports it. However, they lack the ideological, practical, and personal foundations necessary for that. This leads us to worry about the future of the United States.

As democratic nations around the world admire and follow the United States, if the central nation itself is in such a position... If God has loved the United States until now, will He continue to love it in the future? This leads us to think in a different direction.

From this perspective, we understand that the United States as a whole is not in a position that God can love at this moment. When we see this, it is needless to say that the countless other nations are even less likely to be in such a position. So, if God cannot love the United States, which has represented the world, what nation could He possibly love?

There are numerous ethnic groups living within the United States. If God cannot love the United States, can He love any specific ethnic group within it, one that represents the world? We find that there is no such ethnic group. If there are no ethnic groups, then are there families that can represent those ethnic groups and the world? We cannot identify any families that could claim to represent the nation or the world.

Then, if we go beyond families to individuals, is there anyone who can truly represent the world and be loved by God? We cannot definitively say that there is. No one can be confirmed as a person who is worthy of God's love. In this light, the question of where individuals, families, ethnic groups, nations, and the world that God can love truly exist becomes a significant issue for us believers today.

From this perspective, if we leave the United States and focus on the Republic of Korea, we find that the situation is similar. With the North and South standing in opposing positions, can God truly love the Republic of Korea? It is impossible for Him to love both countries simultaneously. The Republic of Korea itself is a problem.

When we question whether there is a specific family within the Republic of Korea that can represent the world and be loved by God, we find that we cannot identify such a family here. Even if we set aside families, is there even one individual who can represent the world and be loved by God? We find that we do not know.

Thus, whether we look at the United States, which has represented the world, or Korea, we cannot find a nation that can proudly represent individuals, families, tribes, nations, and the world that God can love. Today, it seems unlikely that such a nation exists in this world. From this perspective, we might conclude that there is no possibility of such a nation existing.

When we return to individuals and reflect on our lives, we must ask whether we, as believers in God and many other religious individuals, are living lives through which we can receive God's love. When we question this, we find that there is no one who can confidently say, "I am a person who can receive God's love throughout my life. I am the one whom God can represent and love among all people in the universe."

As you go through your lives, even those of you who are older, when you reflect on your entire life from the past to the present, can anyone claim that they have lived more time doing good than doing evil? No one can make such a claim.

The battle between good and evil unfolds through our bodies.
If you are in a good position, joy accompanies you. When you encounter good deeds and perform good actions, joy comes to you. So, when we question how much we have been in a position to rejoice on behalf of the entire nation or the entire world, and how much of our personal lives have been lived in a way that God can look upon us with joy, we find that there may only be one, two, or three years of such experiences. We cannot be sure. When we consider whether we have even had a year or just a few months of such experiences, we find that no matter how old a person is, if we ask them, there is no one who can say, "I felt unforgettable joy for even a few months during my entire life." Even if they felt joy, it was only for a moment. When we sum this up, even when considering the lives of people in their 70s or 80s, we must ask how many days they have truly lived joyfully and how much they have stood in positions of the highest value or the highest status. No one can be sure.

On the other hand, we have lived most of our lives with irritation amidst sadness, pain, and adversity. In other words, the majority of our lives have been spent living under conditions that our true selves do not desire. When we consider this, we conclude that we are not people who have lived happily, but rather people who have lived unhappily.

In unhappiness, there can be no happiness. Unhappiness and happiness are opposites. The path to finding happiness is good, and if there is a center that can become the subject of good, it must be God. If God is the ultimate ideal subject and the ultimate subject of good, then I must become someone who can rejoice centered on that God. However, when I realize that I have spent more time in a position of unhappiness than in a position of joy, it testifies to the fact that humanity is in a state of unhappiness. This means that heaven is in a position opposite to happiness, which is why humanity is also in a state of evil and suffering. We cannot deny this.

From this perspective, unhappiness is connected to suffering, and suffering is in opposition to goodness, so you must understand that it is connected to evil. 

Even from an environmental perspective, we can separate ourselves from such environments. When we consider ourselves as individuals, there is the person of the body and the person of the mind. The person of the mind seeks to pursue good deeds, while the person of the body desires and seeks the opposite. Good seeks to go in one direction, while evil obstructs it. We know that this conflict unfolds through our lives. The desires of the mind always clash with the demands of the body. The mind demands goodness, while the body demands the opposite.

Where does goodness begin? Goodness does not start from oneself. When we consider where goodness begins, we see that it cannot start from oneself. Goodness must begin from a place that serves others. It is not about serving oneself, but about serving others. Therefore, when someone becomes a "good person," they are not someone who starts from themselves, but someone who strives to live for others, work for others, and act for others. Such people are universally recognized as "good people" in life or at the moment of death. Thus, we can determine here that goodness does not start from a place of self-interest, but from a place of concern for others.

What is evil? It is the mindset that "everything exists for me. The starting point of everything must be for my sake." This is the position of evil. We must understand how goodness and evil diverge. Goodness remains in the desire to serve others, while evil remains in self-interest. 

When we look at our hearts, we find that our hearts always seek to lead us in a good direction. "Serve others, have compassion for others, sacrifice for others, live for others." This is the path of goodness.

What is the path of evil? It is the opposite. "Let everyone go for me, let everything exist for me." This is where the history of good and evil diverges. We must understand this. However, today, this path is not clear. When we ask what is good and what is evil, many do not know. Goodness is determined by serving others rather than oneself. Evil is the position where others live for me and exist for my sake. From this perspective, we must clearly understand where the divergence between good and evil lies.

My joy must also bring joy to others to be considered good.
From this perspective, we must ask what kind of position allows us to rejoice in our lives. What kind of position can I rejoice in? It is a position where my true nature is fulfilled. When my true nature is fulfilled, it means that when the environment aligns with my desires, I stand in a place where I do not experience depletion and where a good environment is established, I feel joy.

If I impose restrictions or limitations that cause others to suffer, yet still claim to be happy, that is not goodness. The fulfillment of my heart, or true nature, means that the entire environment harmonizes without conflict, and when I rejoice, they also rejoice. No matter how happy I may feel, if the other person expresses sorrow, that is not good. Therefore, the fulfillment of my desires must be something that is good for both me and others.

When individuals do well, they want to boast to those around them. They want to boast when they do well, but they absolutely do not want to boast when they do wrong. What does it mean to do well? It means standing in a position where one can benefit the environment. It is through standing in a position that can benefit the environment that one can boast. If boasting causes harm to others or those around them, then that is connected to evil. Because it is connected to evil, such actions are rejected. From this perspective, we must clearly understand that the standards of good and evil are established. 

To boast, one must stand in a position that is favorable to everyone. To stand in a position that is favorable to everyone, what must be done? One cannot stand in a position welcomed by all by coercing or imposing restrictions. To stand in a position welcomed by all, one must be able to benefit the whole and provide for the whole. Such a subjective position...
When you stand there and boast, that boast becomes an eternal boast. It is not just my boast, but it becomes the boast of everyone and the boast of the entire environment. You must understand that it is only in such a place that goodness truly begins.

For this reason, our conscience, which seeks goodness, always urges us to strive for others. It is only after striving for others that true joy comes. At the end of striving for oneself, there will inevitably be a backlash. When the conscience tells us to sacrifice for others and to exist for the whole, it is clear that what the conscience itself desires is a good position and a good place.

God's Desired World
The heart must be able to control the body in order to walk the path of goodness. On the other hand, the body has no regard for others. When the body is hungry, it demands to eat by any means necessary. It pulls us in the opposite direction. This body commands us to disregard society and everything else, focusing solely on oneself.

From this perspective, we must distinguish between the good and evil standards within ourselves. In other words, the heart should aim towards good places, while the body's desires lead to evil places. We must understand this. The person standing at these two boundaries, those who are in that position, are the very essence of 'me.' Therefore, you must always control your body and guide it in the direction your conscience desires; otherwise, you cannot carve out the path of goodness.

For this reason, without becoming a good person of God, one cannot hope for the family that God desires. Furthermore, without becoming a good family of God, one cannot hope for a good nation or world. Therefore, the most pressing issue is that before resolving these matters in the world, one must find a solution within oneself. What is that boundary? It is the standard of good and evil, and the division of that standard begins from the point where the directions of the heart and body diverge. You must understand this.

Because God is in a good position, God favors those who exist for others. Originally, humans are not born for themselves. You must understand this. People in the world respect themselves more than any other existence in the universe. They wish the universe existed because of them. However, that is not the case. Originally, humans are not born for themselves. Why? Because we ourselves are not causal beings. All beginnings do not start from us. Because they start from some cause, humans are ultimately beings of consequence. Because they are beings of consequence, they cannot determine their position of existence without disregarding the cause.

From the moment of birth, humans must stand in a position that represents the purpose of the causal being and desire relative purposes. Only then, when one thinks about the value of their existence, can they realize that they were not born for themselves. Ultimately, they must understand that they were born for the subject. Because they were born for that subject...

That subject has a purpose. The subject has the purpose of the subject. If there is a first cause as a subject, then there must be some purpose as a subject. We were born as relative beings before the first subject, so this relative being must also have a purpose. Therefore, the purpose of the first cause and the purpose of the relative must not diverge. They must become one. Only in the place where they become one can this purpose become my purpose, the purpose of the object, and also the purpose of the subject. The place where this purpose is fulfilled is where both the object and the subject feel joy. This is what humans should aspire to and live for. When we see God as the first cause, humans are destined to enjoy joy from the position of the object.

Individuals, families, tribes, nations for others
When we look at humans, they are made up of men and women. So why was a man born? Was he born for himself? No. A woman was not born for herself either. A man was born, ultimately, no matter how much he boasts, because of a woman. A woman, no matter how beautiful or accomplished she may be, was not born for herself. She was born because of a man. She was born because of a man.

When we consider the origins of all existence, we can see that no one is born for themselves. Today, humans do not understand this. Today, so-called men think they live as they do because they are great. However, that is not the case. A man must live for a woman. Of course, there may be a relative third purpose in the society that men and women desire, but the most important issue is that a man is not born solely for himself. A woman is also not born solely for herself. It is clear that they were born for each other.

Then, since a man is for a woman and a woman is for a man, what do they desire? People are not born to live only for themselves. There is a family, and if that family is a wonderful family, God hopes that family will become a representative of families on a national level. Suppose there is a couple who claims to have the greatest love in the world. What does that mean? It means they want to become a central family that the entire nation can follow. They want to create a family that the whole world can emulate, right?

Ultimately, where is the purpose of their mutual love? The purpose of wanting to be the best in the world is to determine that central position for the whole and to live for the whole. Today, we do not understand this. Wanting to be the best family is not for the sake of being the best alone. It is to become the standard for the whole. By becoming the standard for the whole, they can bring about the benefit of the whole, which is why the love of the couple also seeks the highest love.

Next, if we consider a tribe, the tribe wishes to become the best tribe in the world. Why do they want to be the best tribe? It is not for the sake of their own tribe alone. They do so to become a model among the tribes of the world. So ultimately, who is it for? It may seem like it is for oneself, but one must understand that it is for the relative environment.

The same goes for a nation. When we think of 'the Republic of Korea,' the Republic of Korea wishes to become the best nation in the world, which is what all thirty million people desire. Why does the Republic of Korea want to be the best nation in the world? We should not wish for it just for our own prosperity. That alone is not enough. The Republic of Korea wants to be the best nation in the world to become a model among many nations. Ultimately, this is not just for the Republic of Korea itself, but it is for the world. We must think that history develops based on this principle.

Today, it is clearly proven that there is not a single truly good person in an individual's lifetime. No one claims, "I live representing my siblings." Why? Because when we look at life as a whole, there are more evil aspects than good. Because of this, there are more evil families than good families. Since families are formed from this, there are more evil tribes than good tribes among many tribes. Isn't that so? Since the world is an extension of the individual, and humanity is an extension of the individual, that is inevitable.

Today, we know that the world we live in has issues such as the democratic world and the communist world. We are facing conflicting, opposing, and contradictory global situations. So what ideology will be able to become the center of the world in the future? That is the question. A nation that pursues only its own interests will perish. Such a nation will inevitably retreat. It retreats based on this principle.

Today, based on this principle, if the United States has become the center of the world, it must remain the center forever. Then the United States will not perish. If the United States has risen to the position of a leading nation in the world by riding the tide of fortune or heavenly fortune, and if we analyze this based on the principles of existence, it is not just for the sake of the United States. It represents the entire ideology that has appeared throughout the historical era, and it has been established as a subject nation that can pursue this in any era, serving as a representative center nation for the world. If the United States has become such a nation, it will not perish. The United States was not established to exist solely for itself. Therefore, we know that the United States has been declining since the 1970s.

Creation is about investing while also finding joy
So why must it be this way? Why must we exist for others? That is the question. You must understand the fundamental issue: why did God create such humans, and why does He desire this human society to form? You must understand this.

Look. To understand this, we must delve into the fundamental issue. If the center of the universe is God, then we must ask why God created heaven and earth. Why did He create humans? Did He create humans for Himself, or for someone else? Today, established churches say, "Ah, God created heaven and earth for the sake of the world He created." It may seem simple, but with that alone, God cannot be a God of love or an ideal God. For whom did He create heaven and earth? He created it for Himself, and also for humans, who can be His counterparts.

No matter how great, absolute, or omnipotent God is, He cannot have good things by Himself. The noun "happiness," or the adjective "good," cannot be established in solitude. There must be a relative relationship for there to be goodness and happiness. Is there anyone who claims to be happy alone? No matter how great God is, even the omnipotent God, try being alone. Would that be happiness? Suppose there is a musician who sings beautifully and sings alone. Is that happiness? There must be a counterpart. There must be give and take for there to be goodness. If I ask you, "Is this true?" you must answer for everything to be resolved. Everything is interconnected. For God to be good, He cannot be alone.

Look. When you read the Bible, it simply states that God created heaven and earth. It says He created everything by His word. When He calls someone, they respond, "Yes." When He says, "Let there be stars," the stars come into being, and when He says, "Let there be this earth," it comes into being. However, we must understand that there is an infinite order and law, and that it has advanced principles that have developed from small to large. After creating all these things, the essence of all things is what is referred to in the Bible as Adam and Eve, the ancestors of humanity.

When this is unfolded, one world runs with masculine qualities, and another runs with feminine qualities. The relationship between man and woman is a horizontal relationship of subject and object. Then what is the relationship between God and humans? It is a vertical relationship of subject and object.

You often say, "That person has a righteous heart." What does it mean to have a righteous heart? There must be a standard by which it is deemed righteous. Where is that standard? Is that standard my heart? Not at all. When you ask how many miles it is from Seoul to Daegu, if someone says it's 700 miles, it must be measured from a starting point. You cannot arbitrarily choose any point as your standard. There must be a standard from which to measure. When we say, "He has a righteous heart," what is that based on? Is it based on my grandfather? My grandmother? My teacher? There must be a standard. To start, there must be a standard. With a starting standard, one must go through a process to achieve a purpose. For example, the standard is the horizon.

Also, when we say, "The conscience is upright," it is indeed upright, but this is said in relation to something vertical. It is like saying, "The tree is straight." This must be determined based on a 90-degree angle centered around the center of 360 degrees. If this angle is off, the center shifts. Do you understand? If this is at 90 degrees and all sides are 90 degrees, it must be 360 degrees; if even slightly off, the center moves. To determine an absolute, eternal, and fixed center, all sides must have the same 90 degrees. Only then will that position be unchanging. Therefore, when we say the conscience is upright, it is evaluated based on human relationships, horizontally, in terms of men and women. When we say it is straight, it is in relation to the world. This is how it is.

So why did God create heaven and earth? You must understand that. The fact that He created means that He invested power. It is an investment of power. Right? It is an investment of power. The investment of power refers to the consumption of the self. No matter how omnipotent God is, if the power He expended does not return, God will be depleted.

When you eat breakfast and engage in labor, you quickly become hungry, right? You quickly become tired, right? Why? Because when you invest power, it becomes a minus for the subject. There is no joy in losing in everything. Goodness must come from a plus. Therefore, God did not create heaven and earth to be sad or unhappy. He created them to be good. Thus, there must be something that can always be plus. Right?

So when do we find that plus? When can we bring it in? This is the issue. There is a standard of completion for the created beings. "Until this time..."
"When you invest, it will return from that moment." This is the same with business, right? "If I put in this much effort, then I will gain this much." It's the same idea. "If I study hard and pass a certain threshold, then afterwards, I will reap the benefits." We study with this mindset, right? Whether it's for exams or anything else... When you have a desire to achieve something and push past that limit, it will definitely come back to you. This is the law of the universe.

God is the same. If He created humans, then why did He create them? Isn't it because He invested His power? He did invest. He consumed Himself. However, when He completely invests everything centered on humans and reaches the day of completion, it does not escape. On the day of completion, what happens? Afterwards, it returns. We need to think about this principle.

If you invest a hundred and receive something of lesser value in return, God would not have continued His creation. If you invest a hundred, then what you receive should be a hundred, a hundred and ten, two hundred, three hundred, something of a higher dimension in value. It should return as something infinite. When this happens, creation is joyful in the act of investing. Therefore, when we consider how it should return, it must return as something of a higher dimension in value. When it returns with such value, what is it that can bring joy upon its return? That is love. We need to understand this.

Even if one is consumed, the way to find joy is through love. Love does not just happen. Love manifests as a result of completion. When God invests all His power to create humans completely, and when humans are completed and God's investment comes to an end, that individual is completed. When it is completed, what does it return with? It returns with a content of a much higher dimension than the hundred invested. What is the source of this high-dimensional completion? That is love. Do you understand?

If you don't understand this, look at this. When mothers breastfeed their babies, it is like the babies are sucking on a hose attached to their bodies. They are consuming, but where is the parasitic nature in that? Where is the enemy in that? However, when the baby is hungry and drinks eagerly, the mother is just happy and says, "Ah!" Now, why is there such a law in the world? It is strange. Where in the world is there a law where one consumes and is happy?

Where does the power to sustain that consumed self come from? It comes from a loving heart. Do you understand? Only from true love can one sacrifice and find joy in being consumed. You need to know that if this path did not exist, even God Himself could not have been in a position to create the universe and all things.

God is a scientist. If He is a scientist, it may seem strange, but He is the ancestor of science, the ancestor of mathematics. Ultimately, when creating humans, I invest my strength and my whole self, and it may seem like I am left with only a shell, but when it returns, I must discover a self that can completely fill and overflow with what I have invested. This is the conclusion of all theoretical settings. Therefore, for those who seek the path of love, that path is one of investment, and without sacrifice, it cannot be fulfilled. This is the conclusion through the principles of creation. You must understand this clearly. Do you understand? "Yes."

Today, fallen humanity must return through the historical process of recreation, but what is this process of return? It means that we must do again what God was doing. Therefore, just as God went through a sacrificial process of investing all of Himself when creating humans, we, in our journey of recreation and seeking the way of salvation, must also completely invest ourselves to achieve a love that can reap something greater than what we have invested. When this happens, the ideal individuals, families, tribes, and world will emerge. Only then can we find all of this.

Now, isn't it the same for you? When you go to the market and meet neighborhood friends, if a friend asks, "Hey, where are you going?" and you say, "I'm going to the market," and they ask, "Why are you going to the market?" would anyone say, "Why? I'm going to lose ten cents"? If someone goes to the market to lose ten cents, that person is crazy. Is there anyone who would say such a thing? If they said that, they would be considered insane. However, if you say, "I'm going to make a profit of ten cents," then... Everyone needs to understand this. All actions and movements in this world do not operate at a loss. They absolutely do not engage in movements that result in loss. You need to understand this principle.

Based on this principle, when we consider where the ultimate cause of existence lies, why did God create in this way? It is because God Himself exists as an eternal subject for the sake of the object, and thus, we humans are necessary.

When viewed from the perspective of God, He is a personal God. He is like us... He is a subject who can completely communicate with us as individuals. If that is the case, then there must be a moral law that He thinks should govern human life. There must be a law that states how humans should live. Just as there are moral laws and human feelings, there must also be heavenly laws and heavenly feelings in God. Isn't that so? It must be that way. God must have such love as a subject and must have such laws. Furthermore, humans, as objects, must also have those laws and love. However, if there are human morals and feelings but no heavenly laws and feelings, then this is a contradiction.

The place where humans are the happiest is where human morals and feelings, as well as heavenly laws and feelings, become one. So, what is the place of ultimate happiness for humans? It is the place where human morals (人倫) and human feelings (人情), heavenly laws (天倫) and heavenly feelings (天情) are unified. When does such a place come to be? When does that time come? If God created humans as objects, then when can God, as the subject, acknowledge the complete value of that object? That time is when they are mature. You need to understand this. It is the time of maturity. The time when love can be given and received is not in the immature phase but in the mature phase. It cannot be seen any other way. If creation was for the ideal of love, then when will that love meet God? Of course, God loves from the position of the subject as a father, but when can the object recognize the subject? That time is when they are mature.

When a man and a woman mature, they enter adolescence. What is adolescence? It is when they no longer see a man merely as a man. They try to see the man as one who represents the universe. Isn't that so? During adolescence, when women think of men, they try to see them as representatives of the world. Is that true or not? Our young ladies, when they get married in the future, do they want to marry a man who represents the world or one who represents Daegu? What do you think?

In adolescence, there are many romantic notions like "Ah! You are the eternal flower of love." They express love with grand adjectives that ordinary people cannot even touch. In adolescence, they no longer think of Daegu. They look at the Republic of Korea and the world. At that time, everyone becomes a poet and a writer. They want to take the whole world and place it in their hearts, and they want to embrace the ocean and walk with it.

Therefore, youth is a wonderful time. Why is it a wonderful time? Because as the horizontal subject and object meet, and as they get closer to each other, the vertical relationship between God and humanity also comes closer. Do you understand what I mean? This is how it happens. When a man and a woman mature and try to bind themselves together with true love, all the investment that God made in creation will bear fruit, and they will become one and finally return. Ultimately, this means that human love must become one with God's love. The laws of human morality must align with the standards of heavenly morality.

Has such a point appeared in the history of humanity today? If such a point had appeared, God would have smiled. Wouldn't He? Would God have cried or been happy? When we consider the ancestors of humanity, there was one man and one woman. Isn't that right? Then who was there? There was one God who could be a father, one who could be a master. In our Unification Church, we also believe there were angels. So, with only these four beings, God created.

Now, would God have made these two people just to be happy with each other? God, being lonely Himself, created them. If I am here talking and sweating without anyone else around, wouldn't that make me a crazy person? Yes? Because you are here, we can exchange words, and as this continues to multiply, the realm of that relationship widens, and the more it widens, the better it becomes. Isn't that so? Isn’t that so? The uproar that happens without reason is because you must do this to survive. Therefore, you will surely become a group that survives.  
When you become such a group, you will stand at the forefront where you can inherit the world that God desires, passing through families, clans, races, nations, and the world. Because such an automatic conclusion has been reached, for those living in Gyeongsang-do, you already know that world and have been shown the way to go, so please do not get tired. Do you understand? "Yes." Now, until the day the teacher goes, let’s not get tired and go with determination. Do not become absolute losers. Do not become traitors. Do you understand? "Yes." Do not die but survive, and we must restore the nation we desire. Isn’t that right? "Yes."  
If you cannot do that, you must become someone who can say, "If I die, I will leave a will that can continue to exist. If there is no place to leave that will, I will plant it in the heart of my comrades and return."  
You must understand that this is the principle of the tradition that remains in the Unification Church today, and by stepping forward into a position that receives God's trust, you will surely become the sons and daughters that God desires, which is why I have spoken like this today.  
<Prayer> Father, this is Daegu. Looking back on nearly 20 years of history, it feels like just yesterday when we were criticized as a group of heretics in this city. I cannot forget the years when we were persecuted everywhere and chased away from door to door. However, I do not hold a grudge against established churches. I realize how much you have suffered on this path, and I am grateful for the opportunity to step into your heart.  
During that time, they have all become exhausted. We must not become exhausted as well. At that time, they were thriving, but as time flows, the fortunes of the world have changed, and we have come to a stage where we can take the offensive. In this situation, we must be strong and courageous.  
God, who knew that Moses, whom Joshua and Caleb supported, would fall in the wilderness, raised up weak and young Joshua and Caleb to lead the Israelite people a second time, and I believe the message given to them was to "be strong and courageous."  
May the hearts of the young boys and girls gathered here, the hearts of the youth, the hearts of the adults, and the hearts of the elderly be filled with the strength of the chosen people. We must be stronger and more courageous in facing the global satanic realm. Like Caleb and Joshua, who were filled with hope for the nation of Israel, we are in a position to gather the second foundation of the Israelite people, which is our current reality.  
Even if the first-generation leaders have all fallen, it is now the responsibility of the second generation to take charge, and I know that this is the mission of the Unification Church today. The mission remains for the young people with hidden hearts for heaven throughout the three thousand ri to bring them back before heaven by making them repent on the new foundation of their ancestors, so it is time for us to engage in a dual strategy. It is not a fight with swords and guns but a way to overcome through God's strategy, through sacrifice and death, and through the path of uniting with a loving heart, we have endured the long years.  
Finally, we have reached the national limit. Now, even if the path to the world’s limit is miserable, we know that we cannot let go of this fateful path, and because we know that God is more miserable than we are, we must go. We must raise our eyes and look at the mountains and fields of Gyeongsangnam-do and Gyeongsangbuk-do. We must look at all the peaks where nations intersect.  
Just as God informed Elijah that there are over 7,000 who have not bowed down to Baal among the Christian world, we know that there are over 7,000 who have not compromised in the satanic world. Therefore, we are strengthening our strength and sincerity to pave the way and reach out to the world, so may you look upon the future path of the Unification Church with compassion and protect it.  
Father, the children here have sworn to protect the homeland. They have sworn to uphold the dignity and face of the sovereign homeland more than any foreign country, so please do not let them forget that oath. They have not taken responsibility because someone urged them but have volunteered to fight, so please allow them to fulfill their responsibilities and push the fate of America toward Korea. I ask that I may come and praise their efforts, and may the future generations and descendants of the world bow their heads for Korea, allowing them to transcend traditional ideological worlds and fulfill their historical mission.  
As we have been entrusted by heaven until now, may we be allowed to go until the time when we can return, and may we be able to go forward without doubt. I earnestly ask that the day of freedom, peace, and the sacrifice of God's love may come soon, where we can serve and be loyal to you on this earth.  
In front of the remaining history and the remaining world, may we hasten the busy long road we must go day and night, and may the mission of this church, which cannot rest until we reach the grave, shine brightly forever.  
May the path of sovereignty be remembered forever, and may we be allowed to connect the lines of contact so that the earth can remain filled with loyalty and zeal.  
I ask once again that you protect us with your infinite love until we meet again, and I pray all these words in the name of the True Parents. Amen.  
2)  
The Path of True Glory  
<Prayer> Beloved Father, today is November 5, 1972, the first Sabbath of this month. May your glory, mercy, and praise shine forever this morning.  
According to the ties of life, you have made all people your children, and according to the ties of creation, you have established all creation as the footstool of your victory. I hope that you will fulfill this holy mission according to your will and take sole authority.  
From the time you encountered the fallen ancestors of humanity, you have traced the painful history of restoration, Father, and we know how much you have been denied before individuals and before nations and countries. You must have wanted to give up on humanity that denies you, but still, we bow down and give thanks before your mercy and love as you have endured while looking forward to the time of your desire. We must realize that the fact that humanity, which should have perished, has survived until now is a reflection of the infinite grace you have permitted.  
Father, now the ultimate point of the end of the century is approaching us. Now, I realize that the existence of "I" has no power to resolve my own fate. The path of individual victory must go through the nation, the path of national victory must go through the world, and the path of world victory must connect with the victory of heaven and the Father. We are facing a decisive era that cannot be separated from your victory. As this breathless scene approaches us, we think that if we do not stand in a position that can align with the purpose you desire, we will become pitiful beings, and the nation and world will become pitiful as well. Therefore, we must long for you with sincerity, and we must discover ourselves that can solemnly strive toward the ultimate destination.  
We know that there is a conflict between the evil world and the good world. Born as descendants of evil people in an evil land, we must clear the path we have walked in evil and enter the path of goodness, which is the path of restoration.  
Since there is no way back, that path must be a path of suffering. When we think that the way is blocked by individuals, families, nations, and the world, and even by the authority of Satan who holds the power of the air, the thought of retracing this throughout our lives becomes increasingly close to impossibility. The more we think about it, the more we realize that we have the duty and responsibility to overcome this path, even if it means risking our lives.  
No matter how high the mountain we must cross, when we think that our ancestors perished and that all our forefathers’ nations could not cross this peak, we know that we must make the greatest resolution in history as we run toward this summit. Therefore, we must love you with all our hearts, minds, and sincerity. Before you, we must be crazy. We must become one with you. Since it is a path that cannot be crossed with our own strength, we are hoping for the strength of heaven.  
We realize that you have come to us to help us overcome the suffocating path of restoration. In this place where we are raising our hands to seek the gifts you have permitted, or in this place where we are heading toward the summit, may you manifest yourself. We know that your desire throughout history has been for us to raise a history of possibility at this impossible stage, so we are hoping to become sons and daughters who can overcome this and be worthy of your pride and love.  
While the place of longing may be easy, we must realize that to transcend reality, we must make a decision of life and death, and we must conclude the final battle. As we reflect on whether we have the proper mental attitude and whether we are physically equipped, the more we reflect, the more we realize our shortcomings and our nakedness. Therefore, Father, please clothe our bodies with your strength and power, and unify our hearts with your heart. When we realize that we cannot pledge to overcome victory without becoming your substantial entity, we must understand that if we cannot do so, there is no more pitiful and miserable group than us.  
Because we stand at the highest point before Satan, we are in a position to cooperate maximally before heaven, and we know that it is a place where defeat and victory intersect. When we stand in a place of defeat, we realize that we become enemies before heaven, and we know that it is a place we must not lose. May this time be a time to firmly recognize that each of us has the responsibility to bring about the results of victory and to surpass the standards you have believed in.  
Once again, we are welcoming November through your will. We have this month of 1972 and December remaining. We must fight vigorously during the remaining approximately 55 days. As we transition from 1972 to welcome 1973, Father, I earnestly hope that we can appear on the global stage with a new heavenly victory, becoming a group that you govern.  
Before us, not only individuals but also parents, siblings, relatives, nations, and the world connected to the evil world are running. We must take the center of heaven's will and serve as a locomotive representing heaven's heart. When we think that the speed of running is determined by the strength of the locomotive, we must run at all times. We must not lack strength. I earnestly hope that we can be aware of the mission of the locomotive that knows how to run with a strong and persistent attitude.  
Now that your beloved children have bowed before your presence, may you call each one by name. You were called from this place, and when you came this way, there were many times when you could not stand or remain, but coming this far is due to the grace of heaven that has protected and nurtured you. Please allow us to discover ourselves who can once again give thanks before heaven. May we realize how heavy the responsibility entrusted to us before heaven is. And may we be allowed to become children who can make a new resolution centered on heaven.  
If you cannot come to us now, please let us know all of this. May you dwell deeply in our hearts as a connection of life and be present among us. Is it not the great wish of history to anticipate the day when you can govern all of us? Now we must become gentle and humble like children. We must become naked children. We must become true heirs who cannot leave your embrace, so please allow us to be such sons.  
Knowing that I shed tears because I realized that I could not cry for the first time while looking at my parents' faces, is it not our wish to look at your face with tears on behalf of the joy of all people? We should be able to smile while looking at your face, but instead, we have been smiling at the connections of the satanic world. Now, we wish to break away from this and smile toward you, and we hope to have a parent who can face that smile. It is the heart of these insufficient children to wish to share joy, anger, sorrow, and pleasure with you, so Father, please come to us.  
When we think that there is no one to guard us on this harsh, lonely, and desolate path, we realize that the satanic world rejoices in this, and there are enemies.
각할 때에, 저희들은 고독해도 고독한 모양을 해서는 안 되겠습니다. 아무리 죽음이 엇갈리는 자리에 있다 하더라도 저희들에게는 이를 악물고 극복할 책임이 있습니다. 망해서는 안 될 하늘의 권위와 하늘의 위신과 하늘의 처지와 하늘의 체면이 있다는 것을 생각하게 될 때, 저희 자신들은 언제나 언제나 약한 자리에, 언제나 언제나 주저하는 자리에, 언제나 언제나 후퇴하는 자리에 있어서는 안 되겠습니다.  
전진! 전진! 전진! 죽어 쓰러지는 한이 있더라도, 원수들이 과연 과연 하늘의 아들이라고 마을 마을을 통하여 기억에 증거를 남기고 갈 수 있는 당신의 아들딸들이 되게 허락하여 주옵기를 간절히 바라옵고 원하옵니다.  
아버님, 이제 1972년도 막바지에 처해 있습니다. 대한민국이 갈 길을 아버지께서 책임져 주셔야 되겠습니다. 이 나라, 이 민족의 지도자는 그 누구도 아니었습니다. 남북이 엇갈리는 이런 실정 가운데 있어서 참의 길을 모색하여 아버님을 시봉할 수 있는 무리가 이 땅 위에 없어서는 안 될 것을 생각하게 되옵니다. 아버님이여, 여기에 모인 저희들은 남한 땅에서도 북한 땅에서도 당신을 대신하여 설 수 있는 그날이 오기를 바라고 있습니다. 아버지여, 인도하여 주시옵소서.  
악과 선이 교차되는 현시점에 있어서, 선이 선 될 수 있는 위치를 지키기 위해서는 아버님이 이끌어 가고 대해 주시지 않으면 안 된다는 것을 생각하게 될 때, 온갖 정성과 모든 것을 아버지 앞에 다 바쳐야 할 이때인 것을 각자가 새로이 명심하여 이때를 놓치는 무리들이 되지 말게 하여 주시옵기를 간절히 바라옵고 원하옵니다.  
아버지여, 이 땅 위에 기독교의 이름을 가지고 왔다 갔던 수많은 애혼들이 있는 것을 알고 있사오니, 그들을 해방시켜 주시옵소서. 수많은 종교의 이름을 가지고 이 땅에 왔다가 희생된 무리들이 있사오니, 그들을 해방시켜 주시옵소서. 한 나라의 충신으로서 절개를 지키기 위하여 희생되어 간 사람도 많사오니, 이날 이 아침에 그들을 용납하여 주시옵소서. 그들을 해방시켜 주시옵소서. 사사로운 생활 가운데서 선을 지지하다가 이 땅 위의 생애를 마치고 간 수많은 백성들이 있사오니, 아버지, 그들을 해방시킬 수 있는 은사를 허락하여 주시옵소서.  
그리하여 영계에서부터 땅까지, 수많은 영인들로부터 후손까지 해방의 은사를 허락하여 주시옵소서. 위로부터 풀지 않고는 아래가 풀릴래야 풀릴 수 없다는 사실을 저희들은 알았습니다. 이것은 땅 위에서 풀어 주어야 된다는 것을 생각하게 될 때에, 지금까지 이 땅에 왔다 갔던 의에 속하는 반열에 섰던 수많은 무리들을, 아버지여, 축복하여 주시옵소서. 그들이 아버지 앞에 갈 수 있는 공인된 길을 오늘 이 시간을 통하여서 허락하여 주시기를 간절히 바라옵고 원하옵니다.  
이제 영계에서 통일교회를 위하여 수고하는 영인들 위에 복을 베풀어 주시옵소서. 그들의 공덕을 치하하여 주시옵소서. 땅을 대신하여 협조하는 모든 것이 당신의 영광의 터전 앞에 자랑이 되고 당신의 마음 가운데 감사의 조건으로 남아질 수 있다는 것을 알고 있사오니, 그들을 축복하여 주시옵소서.  
아버지여! 통일교회 교인들이 이 땅 위에서 충성하는 이상으로 충성하거든 그들도 동참할 수 있는 혜택권 내에 참석시켜 주시옵기를, 아버지, 간절히 바라옵고 원하옵니다. 그리하여 1972년도에는 이 땅에 왔다 갔던 수많은 선한 영인들을 규합하여 지상에 새로운 대열로 포진을 시키고 이북을 향하여 악의 세력을 몰아낼 수 있는 아버지의 권고와 지휘가 같이 하여 주시옵기를 간절히 바라옵고 원하옵니다.  
오래지 않은 날을 남기고 저희들이 나뉘어지는 그런 시간이 오더라도 당신의 뜻과 당신을 사랑하는 데 있어서는 변치 말게 허락하여 주옵고, 멀어지면 멀어질수록 하늘과의 인연을 높일 줄 알고 심정의 깊은 곳에서 하늘과 더불어 맺을 수 있는 사연을 지니는 무리들 되게 허락하여 주시옵기를 간절히 바라옵니다. 만나야 할 무리, 또 만나기를 바라고 있는 그들이 하늘을 중심삼고 기쁠 수 있는 내적 인연을 세계 앞에 옮겨 주기 위하여 만나고 헤어지는 무리들이 되게 하여 주시옵기를 간절히 바라옵니다.  
일본에서 지금 싸우고 있는 당신의 어린 자녀들을 기억하여 주시옵소서. 어려운 일을 치르기 위해 얼마나 수고하고 있다는 사실을 기억하시사, 영계에 있는 수많은 영인들도 협조하게 허락하여 주시옵소서. 그리하여 당신이 원하는 뜻을 세계에 연결시켜 주시옵기를 간절히 부탁드리고 원하옵니다.  
아버지, 각자 개인 개인의 모습을 바라보시고 그 이름을 불러 소명을 하시사 남기신 민족적 사명 앞에, 남기신 복귀의 세계 앞에 부끄러움의 자리에 서는 불쌍한 무리들이 되지 말고, 당신의 칭찬과 자랑과 사랑을 직접 받는 영광의 반열에 참여할 수 있는 무리로서 남아지게 허락하여 주옵기를 간절히 바라옵고 원하옵니다.  
전체를 맡으시옵소서. 1972년도의 후반기를 당신의 뜻 가운데서 처리하여 주시옵소서. 모든 말씀 참부모님의 이름으로써 아뢰었사옵나이다. 아멘.  
<말 씀> 우리는 우리 개인들의 일생을 총망라해 보게 될 때, 참된 일, 혹은 참된 사정, 혹은 참된 생활이 얼마나 있었느냐 할 때, 많지 못한 것을 알고 있습니다.  
타락한 세상에서 슬픈 생활을 하고 있는 인간  
하루의 생활 가운데서 참된 일이 얼마나 있었느냐? 혹은 일년에, 혹은 십년에, 일생에 얼마나 있었느냐 하는 것을 따지고 묻게 된다면, 일생에 있어서, 그야말로 몇 시간, 혹은 몇 개월이나 있었겠느냐 하는 것이 문제가 되는 것입니다.  
참된 결과가 나타나게 되면 기쁨이 따르게 마련입니다. 그렇기 때문에 일상생활에 있어서 우리가 얼마나 기쁜 생활을 했느냐 하는 문제를 두고 볼 때, 어느 누구든지 나는 기쁘게 산다고 하는 사람은 없다는 것을 우리는 결론지어도 과언이 아닌 것입니다.  
이러한 관점에서 볼 때, 대다수의 사람들은 슬픈 자리에 살고 있는 것이 틀림없습니다. 그 슬픔이 결국은 내가 발전할 수 있는 길과 내가 바라는 길과 하나된 자리가 아니라, 그 길과 반대되는 자리에 있다는 사실을 증거하는 것이기 때문에, 슬픈 그 자리는 결국은 괴로운 자리요, 그 자리는 악과 통할 수 있는 자리인 것은 틀림없는 것입니다.  
이러한 관점에서 우리의 생애를 놓고 볼 때, 내가 기쁨과 혹은 참됨과 선한 자리에 얼마나 서서 살았느냐 하고 묻는다면 나는 그렇게 살았다고 할 사람이 없다는 것입니다. 혹시 있다 하더라도 잠깐, 지나가는 한 순간에 지나지 않는 것입니다. 그것이 자리를 잡아 뿌리를 내리고, 줄기와 가지와 잎을 내어 ‘나는 이렇게 무성하다.’할 수 있는 사람은 없다는 것입니다.  
그런 사람이 없다면 그런 가정도 없는 것이요, 그런 씨족, 민족도 없는 것이 아니냐. 그런 사람들이 세계적으로 전개된 것이 인류가 아니더냐. 그 인류로 형성된 것이 국가가 아니더냐. 그 국가들로 이루어 놓은 것이 현재, 2대 조류를 중심삼아 가지고 부딪치고 있는 이 세계 정세가 아니더냐. 이런 문제를 두고 볼 때, 이 세계를 악한 세계라고 전체적으로 결론지어도 과언이 아닌 것입니다. 이처럼 이 세계는 악한 세계이기 때문에, 결국은 타락한 세계라는 것입니다. 타락한 세계가 틀림없다는 것을 우리는 알고 있는 것입니다.  
기독교의 성경을 보면 창세기에서 인간이 타락했다는 것을 가르쳐 주고 있습니다. 인간의 조상이 타락한 조상으로 시작되었기 때문에 타락한 조상으로 말미암아 타락한 부모가 생겨났습니다. 타락한 가정이 생겨났기 때문 에 타락한 자녀와 타락한 씨족, 타락한 민족, 타락한 국가와 세계가 자연히 생겨날 수밖에 없었습니다. 이렇게 해서 생긴 세계는 불행한 세계요, 죄악된 세계요, 타락한 세계입니다.  
타락했다는 명사 그 자체가 떨어졌다는 것이 아니냐. 정상적인 자리에 있지 못하다는 말이 아니냐. 그러면 떨어지는 데 있어서는 얼마만큼 떨어졌느냐 하는 문제를 두고 볼 때, 보통 사람이 상상할 수 없을 만큼 떨어졌다는 것입니다. 높은 하늘이 있다면 그 하늘과 지극히 반대되는 제일 낮은 곳에 떨어졌을 것입니다. 물건이 떨어지게 되면 제일 깊은 곳에 떨어지게 마련입니다. 아무리 태평양 바다가 깊다 하더라도 모래 한 알이 떨어지게 되면 그 물을 뚫고 맨 밑창, 깊은 곳에 떨어져 거기에 머무는 것이 아니냐. 제일 깊은 곳에 떨어지면 제일 깊은 곳에 머무를 것입니다. 제일 높은 하늘이기 때문에 거기에 반대되는 제일 깊은 곳에 떨어질 것이 아니냐.  
그러면 그 떨어진 거리를 두고 볼 때에 우리가 바라는 제1단계의 소원은 어디가 될 것이냐? 태평양 바다라고 한다면 거기에서 떨어진 돌의 희망의 출발 기점을 찾는다면 그곳은 물과 접하는 경계선일 것이 아니냐.  
타락한 인간의 갈 길  
그렇다면 우리 인간으로서 소원할 수 있는 것은 뭐냐? 인간이 어디에 소망을 두고 가다가 미치지 못하고 떨어졌기 때문에, 인간의 소망의 출발점은 어디냐 하면, 그 떨어지기 직전의 선입니다. 그 선을 넘어서는 것이 인간의 소망으로서 바랄 수 있는 출발점이 되는 것은 불가피한 것입니다.  
그 점을 바라보고 가다가 떨어졌기 때문에 그 점을 다시 찾아가지 않으면 안 될 필연적인 운명에 놓여진 것이 타락한 인간의 정상이요, 세계 인류가 가야 할 사정이 아니겠느냐. 그것은 틀림없는 것입니다.  
인간의 소원은 어디서부터 벌어지느냐? 타락선을 넘는 데서부터입니다. 그것은 당연한 말인 것입니다. 그러면 떨어진 우리가 자체적으로 올라갈 수 있겠느냐? 자체적으로 올라갈 수 있는 힘을 가졌다면 좋겠지만 우리 자체들로서는, 떨어진 자체들로서는 다시는 올라갈 길이 없는 것입니다. 떨어진 자가 다시 올라가기 위해서는 어떻게 해야 되느냐? 반대로 끌어주는 힘을 갖추는 일을 하는 사람이 있든가, 그렇지 않으면 땅이 솟구쳐 올라오든가, 그 길밖에 없는 것입니다. 누가 나서서 반대로 끌어 주는 한 사람이 나타나거나, 그렇지 않으면 땅이 솟구쳐 올라오는 천지의 대변동이 있기 전에는 그 떨어진 구렁텅이에서 본연의 자리를 찾아 올라올 길이 없는 것 입니다.  
이와 같이 떨어진 인간들을 보고 있는 어떤 한 분이 계시다면, 그분이 떨어진 자체를 두고 볼 때에, 자기가 넉넉히 구할 수 있는 능력을 가진 사람이라면 구해 줄 수 있을 것입니다. 그렇지만 그러한 사람을 건져 주고 난 후에 하나에서부터 열까지 손해난다면 안 구해 주는 것입니다. 구해 줄래야 구해 줄 수 없는 입장에 설 것이 아니냐. 구해 주되, 그 떨어진 자가 구해 주는 사람으로 하여금 무슨 소망의 내적 이익을 줄 수 있다면 건져 줄 수 있는 길이 있을지 모르지만, 그렇지 않으면 떨어져 있는 것을 보더라도 구해 줄 수 없는 것이 아니냐. 그런 입장에 선 것이 인류가 아니겠느냐, 우리 인간들이 아니겠느냐 하는 것을 생각해 보게 될 때, 그런 것이 내가 아니냐 하는 문제를 생각해 보게 될 때, 내 갈 길은 어디냐, 인간이 가야 할 길은 어디겠느냐 하는 것이 문제가 되는 것입니다.  
아무리 옆으로 돌아가고 옮겨 간다 하더라도 그것은 태평양 바다 가운데서 이동하는 것에 지나지 않는 것이 아니냐. 그것은 이동하나마나 한 것과 마찬가지의 움직임입니다.  
그렇기 때문에 여기에서 인생의 갈 길이 문제되는 것입니다. 갈 길에 있어서 단 한 가지 방법이 있는데 그것은 어떻게 가야 하느냐? 옆으로는 아무리 노력을 하고 아무리 왕래하더라도 그 사람의 갈 길은 절망으로 끝날 것입니다. 그것은 망하는 운세에 사로잡힐 것은 두말할 필요도 없는 것입니다. 단 한 가지 희망을 가질 수 있는 것은 그 자리를 떠나야 하는 것입니다. 그가 서 있는 자리를 떠나서 도약을 하는 것입니다. 비약을 하는 것 입니다.  
비약을 하는 데는 각도가 좋아야 된다 이겁니다. 어떤 각도를 가지고 무한히 반대의 길로 솟구쳐 올라가는 길밖에 없지 않느냐. 솟구쳐 올라가는 데는 한 점을 중심삼아 가지고 사방, 동서남북 사방을 중심삼아 가지고, 동으로 각도를 갖추어 솟구쳐 올라가는 사람도 있을 것이고, 어떤 사람은 서로 북으로 남으로 자기 나름대로 방향을 갖추어 올라가려고 할 것입니다. 거기에는 천태만상의 길이 있는 것입니다. 안 그렇겠어요?  
동서남북, 사방을 중심삼고 보면 360도를 중심삼아 가지고 평면적보다도 더 많은 각도의 방향을 중심삼아 가지고 그 차이에 의해 자기 나름대로 몸부림을 치며 여기서 도약, 혹은 비약하여 해방을 맞기를 고대하고 있는 인간들임에 틀림이 없는 것이 아니냐. 여러분도 그 어떤 분야의 방향을 갖추어 가지고 어떠한 각도를 향해 수고하고 노력하는 인간이 아니냐. 그렇기 때문에 뭔가, 스스로도 모르지만 해방을 추구하고 있는 것이 인간입니다.  
고통과 어려움 가운데 사로잡힌 자기의 인생고에 부대껴 가지고 그것을 초월하고, 거기에서 해방할 수 있는 한 날이 오기를 진심으로 고대한 것이 역사 이래의 인간상이 아니었더냐. 그 인간상 가운데서 내가 나를 중요시하고 나를 빼놓고는 전체의 가치를 시인하려 하지 않는 그런 자신을 두고 볼 때에, 이 자신이 머물 수 있는 자리와 가야 할 길이 어디겠느냐 하는 문제는 심각한 문제가 아닐 수 없는 것입니다.  
그러면 여러분은 어떠한 자리에 떨어져 있습니까? 거기에는 천태만상의 차이가 있습니다. 선한 조상도 있고 악한 조상도 있기 때문에, 역사 이래 제일 악한 조상이라면 제일 깊은 자리에 있는 것을 말하는 것이요, 역사 이래 제일 선한 조상이라면, 그 조상들의 죽은 사체가 혹은 뼈가 쌓이고 쌓여 그것이 높아져 가지고 하나의 터전으로 남겨졌으면 그 위에 태어난 조상은 선한 자리에 설 수 있는 것입니다.  
악한 조상은 그 뼈라도 천지가 보고 싶어하지 않는 것입니다. 어떤 주인이 있다든가 혹은 어떤 사람이라 하더라도, 악한 사람의 무덤은 바라보고 싶어하지 않습니다. 악한 사람의 행적을 기억하고 싶지 않은 것이 우리 인간의 마음이라 할진대는, 악한 사람의 무덤이라든가 악한 사람의 그 무엇은 남기고 싶어하지 않고 없어지기를 원하기 때문에 맨 밑창에 머물게 되는 것입니다.  
이러한 상하 고저의 차이에 있어서 천태만상의 이런 배경과 역사적 인연을 남기고 있고 또 그것을 지니고 있는 것이 우리 인간임에 틀림이 없는 것입니다.  
남을 위해 희생하라는 뜻  
그러면 자고로 수많은 인간들이 참을 추구하고, 공의를 추구하고, 전체를 위해 희생하고, 전체를 위해서 자기가 빚지기를 원치 않는 것은 무엇 때문이냐? 남에게 줘라, 남에게 이익을 줘라, 빚을 지고 남에게 보탬을 줘라 하는 것은 무엇이냐? 인간은 자기가 어떠한 자리에 있는가 하는 것을 모르기 때문입니다. 수평으로 본다면 자기가 높고 낮음을 모르기 때문입니다.  
그러면 그러한 입장에 선 인간이 왜 남을 위해서 희생해야 되느냐? 결국 좋은 일을 하는 것은, 갑이라는 사람에게 좋은 일이 되었으면 갑이라는 사람이 나를 기억해 주게 됩니다. 기억해 준다는 것은 보이지 않는 줄로 얽어매는 것과 마찬가지입니다. 내가 어려움을 당하더라도 을이라는 사람을 위해서 희생하고 협조했다면 그와 나 사이에 줄을 걸어 놓은 것과 마찬가지입니다. 그것이 자기에게 귀한 것일수록 입체성을 갖는 것입니다.  
덜 가치 있는 것, 덜 귀한 것, 자기가 좋아하지 않는 것을 남에게 주는 것은 절대 선한 것이 못 되는 것입니다. 내가 올라가야 할 운명 길 앞에 조금도 도움이 안 되는 것입니다. 내가 좋아하고 귀중히 여기는 것은 높은 곳에 있기 때문에, 그 높은 곳에 있는 좋은 것을 주게 되면 그 높은 인연을 중심삼고 얽어매는 것과 마찬가지입니다.  
많은 사람을 위해서 내가 희생하면 상대가 많기 때문에, 나는 모르지만 상대의 수많은 선한 조상들이 그 후손들을 협조하기 때문에, 그 높은 자리의 조상들이 후손을 협조해 주는 자리에 서면 나는 그 높은 자리에 있는 후손과 줄을 맨 것과 마찬가지가 되는 것입니다. 그렇기 때문에 그 후손이 이동하게 되면 자연히 나는 끌려가게 마련입니다. 이렇게 되는 것입니다.  
그렇기 때문에 선한 일을 하라고 하는 것은 결국, 무엇을 바라 가지고 하라고 하는 것이냐 하면 내가 높이 갈 수 있는 길을 찾기 위한 하나의 방법입니다.
is the result of fragrance. It speaks of the reality of humans who struggle to seek this. If I give what is left over and not good, it is rather a connection with the bottom, so I cannot rise. Therefore, those who pursue the path of virtue and goodness teach not to owe anything to others. They teach to sacrifice for others. People have a vague belief that those who have a good heart and sacrifice will eventually be rewarded, although they may not know the specific details. However, we know that this has become a uniform educational goal centered around human morality today and has become a goal of culture. Why is that? Because from a fallen position, one hopes for a higher point, and heaven inevitably cannot teach such things in a detailed one-on-one manner, so it teaches symbolically or metaphorically in secret. We must recognize that what has been taught in this way is the call to do good today, to engage in good deeds.

For this reason, giving what I can no longer use to others ultimately becomes a condition that pulls me down to the bottom if the recipient receives it with a true and joyful heart, which is why religions or the world of virtue teach not to do such things today. This can be viewed in this way.

You do not know what position you stand in at this moment. Because you do not know that, humans today are searching for good teachers. When you go to school, who is the best teacher? No matter how knowledgeable someone is and how well they teach with their words, if they are a teacher whose actions or character cannot be emulated, that teacher is not liked. They may listen to the words but laugh behind their back. Are they not seeking a teacher of character? Even regarding their own parents, they prefer parents who love them more than anyone else. Why? Because if there are parents who can give love, and those parents truly love, that truth brings them closer to heaven. Isn’t that right?

Therefore, today, humans desire excellent teachers, and furthermore, if there is an excellent leader who represents heaven centered around their spiritual connections, they demand such a leader. 

Thus, throughout human history, even though we humans did not want it, as long as heaven exists, it has always sent excellent leaders and great prophets to guide and teach during those times. This has been present in the historical era of any nation.

When making friends, people want good friends; when having children, they want good sons and daughters; when men and women marry, they want good husbands and good wives. Everyone seeks what is good. What does good connect with? It connects with truth. Without a good environment, one cannot stand in a true position, so the heart that desires truth aligns with the heart that desires goodness, which we know very well through our daily lives.

Do we need patriots or saints?

From this perspective, who has been the greatest leader representing humanity throughout history? There are patriots representing a nation. In the Republic of Korea, when we mention "General Yi Sun-sin," he is honored as a representative patriot whom our people can commemorate. However, did he love the world as well as his country? He became a patriot but does not reach the ranks of great men or sages. He is a representative patriot of Korea but not a representative of humanity.

Patriots emerge during times of national crisis and turmoil. In normal times of peace, patriots do not appear. It is only when a nation faces the fate of collapse or prosperity, confronting an enemy country that seeks to swallow it, that patriots emerge from the position of defeating and subjugating that enemy. Alternatively, patriots arise from situations where treacherous individuals are rampant and must be eliminated. The term patriot is established in the context of fighting and winning against enemies during difficult times.

In this light, a patriot of one nation becomes an enemy of another nation. Isn’t that so? General Yi Sun-sin is considered a patriot in Korea, but he is not viewed as a patriot in Japan. So, can we say that all Koreans are better than all Japanese? We cannot say that. There may be many good people in Japan compared to bad people in Korea. History unfolds in such a way.

So, do we need patriots or saints? What is a saint? A patriot of one nation fights for the ultimate fate of that nation, while a saint is someone who fights not just for one nation but for the world. Can one become a saint in front of humanity just by fighting for the world? To be recognized as a saint by heaven, one must fight for heaven. Therefore, when we ask who has fought for heaven on behalf of humanity, it is the religious leaders.

Then, what is God’s wish? It is God’s will to represent the entire world; therefore, if there is someone who represents all of humanity and fights for heaven, that person is a being of hope for humanity that can remain in the historical era, and if heaven exists, they must be an inevitable existence that heaven recognizes.

Through the thoughts or actions of such a person, humanity seeks something better than any good friend, better than any good teacher, better than any good patriot, seeking someone who surpasses the great figures of the world representing humanity. If there is a heaven with a history, it is the inevitable desire of humans to seek a true owner who represents the entire historical era of heaven. For this reason, heaven has raised such individuals as representatives of the historical era. This is the role of religious leaders. However, it is strange that these religious leaders are not only standing as religious leaders but also bear the name of saints.

When we speak of saints, we refer to the four great saints. When we mention Jesus, what kind of saint was he? Did he come to this earth and conduct activities centered on the sovereignty of a nation during his thirty years of life? Did he go to war and establish the authority of victory with weapons? He suffered from the moment he was born. He was a man who was chased from the time he was born, not only during his three years of public life. Was he not a pitiful man wandering from one village to another? Eventually, he was cornered by his nation, by Judaism, and by Rome, choosing the path of death that he could not escape. That is the reality.

In a place where anyone else would have fled, Jesus said, “Abba, Father, if it is possible, let this cup pass from me; yet not what I want, but what you want.” This shows that he valued heaven’s will over his own will, indicating that he observed an inner world that was more rewarding than any other saint. To abandon his own will and follow heaven’s will is to represent humanity. He did not represent the Israelite nation, nor Judaism, nor Rome. Standing in such a position means standing in a place of conflict. If he sided with them, he would oppose heaven, and if he sided with heaven, he would oppose them, leading to the need for a judgment of righteousness between these conflicting sides. Wasn’t the prayer in the Garden of Gethsemane about that struggle? This is a profound issue.

The will of his own is a common attitude of heart representing humanity in a fallen world, while the will of heaven is the will that has not yet manifested. His own will is already manifested as a past will.

For this reason, he did not cling to the environment that was destined to perish and die, nor did he seek to organize his life; rather, he had a lifelong desire to leave behind heaven’s will on the foundation of his life, which is why he went to the cross to plant that will until his last moment.

Ultimately, the blood Jesus shed was for the purpose of planting God’s will, and the suffering he endured on the cross was also for God’s will. By planting God’s will, it became a seed that sprouted, grew into a stem, and spread its leaves to expand globally. Therefore, heaven must promote the thought that became the seed of life along with global development. Thus, we can conclude that Christianity, established with such motivation, must inevitably become a worldwide religion.

So, who are the saints? They are religious leaders. Among the four great saints, Jesus is included, but what kind of person was Jesus? He was not a man who went mad for his country. He was not someone who went mad to manage the politics of the human world or to stabilize that nation. What was he mad about as he walked the path of death? He was mad for heaven, for the ideal world of the future that had not yet manifested.

Jesus abandoned not only his family but also his nation, his church, and all the conditions that could lead to success in his time. He did not abandon these to find something inferior; he abandoned them to pursue something better. He gave up the most important things to rise up. He did not die to fall down. Ultimately, this was because the heart that desires to rise and the heart that heaven desires to elevate could find a point of contact. That moment is the end time when the world connects. It is the end of the world of death that tormented him. It is the end of all enemies that whipped him. Therefore, the end must come.

Therefore, if you want to become a person of character, you must learn to endure. In an evil world, responding with ten words for every one word spoken is seen as doing well, but a good person endures. So, I say to endure.

Saints are religious leaders. Jesus was one, and so was Buddha. Buddha left his kingdom and chose the world of heaven’s solitude. He abandoned everything.

When we consider this, we can think that a nation is likewise in a similar position, and that God, who is responsible for the providence of restoration, is in the same position.

So, when we look at God, what would be the most important thing for God? It must be the fulfillment of His will. We know that there is nothing more important than fulfilling the will, in other words, completing the ideal of creation. However, the matter of fulfilling the ideal of creation, that is, the necessity to fulfill the will, is not merely a matter that remains as God's own work. The fulfillment of the will is ultimately a matter that is placed in a relative position apart from God, and that is what we must understand here.

Before God created Adam and Eve, He created all things and then placed Adam and Eve in the central position. The question of whether that central being becomes the fruit of victory or not is, of course, God's desire, but it is not a matter that hinges on God Himself; it lies with humanity.

In other words, in order to bestow the achievement of creation upon humanity, it hinges on whether humanity fulfills 5 percent of the responsibility. While 95 percent has already been accomplished by heaven, if humanity cannot fulfill that 5 percent of responsibility, it will lead to the overall failure. However, if humanity can fulfill that responsibility, the overall purpose will be achieved. 

In light of this issue, one of the matters that God may consider important, and the most important among those matters, is the ideal of creation. However, we must understand that whether it is achieved or not lies not with God Himself but with humanity. We must think once again that humanity stands in the position to determine that important matter.

From this perspective, we see that what has made God sad has not been due to God Himself but rather due to the other party, that is, humanity. Therefore, the joy that God can feel also does not come from God Himself but is brought about by humanity. In other words, all good and bad matters concerning God have been brought about not from God Himself but from humanity in a relative position. Thus, the origin of history has also been established in this way.
We must understand what has been established. The concept of the fall refers to the results that have come about from that perspective. Therefore, in God's providence of restoration, we must recognize that the important being who bears the significant responsibility is not God, but rather humanity.

However, when we look at humanity, even in fulfilling 5 percent of the responsibility, the question of whether humanity itself can complete that 5 percent is not solely determined by humanity alone, as we can see from the results of the fall. There exists a relative being known as the archangel, and if that archangel cooperates well with humanity, then humanity can fulfill its responsibilities meaningfully and brilliantly. However, if the cooperation goes awry, then fulfilling human responsibility becomes impossible. To put it simply, humanity has not been able to fulfill its responsibilities because it fell due to the archangel's fall, indicating that the ultimate cause lies with the archangel.

Important Matters
The Role of the Relative in Deciding Important Matters
In this way, we come to understand that in the human world, important matters and significant decisions are not determined solely by oneself but are decided in relation to the world around us. 

Take the issue of Cain and Abel, for example. Whose responsibility is it for Abel to fulfill his duties? Of course, it lies with Abel, but the relative being, Cain, plays a crucial role in determining this. Similarly, after the judgment, Noah's ability to fulfill the purpose of that judgment also depended more on his sons than on himself.

When Abraham was walking the path of fulfilling his mission, it was not solely dependent on him but also on the offering. Looking at Jacob, the decisive factor in whether he could fulfill his mission during his 21 years was not just within himself but in the relative environment. He had to subdue Laban. Furthermore, when Rachel concealed Laban's idols while leaving, if that had been discovered, not only Jacob but the fulfillment of the mission of Jacob's entire family could have completely failed.

From this perspective, it is an undeniable fact that important events and significant matters in the providence of restoration do not solely depend on oneself. The same goes for Moses. Moses did not fail because of himself but because he broke the tablets. John the Baptist's inability to follow Jesus' will was also due to environmental factors rather than his own shortcomings. From a human standpoint, recognizing Jesus, who is a relative younger brother, as the Messiah is not an easy task. Ultimately, we cannot deny that relative factors have always played a role in determining important issues.

Looking at Jesus himself, he did not bear the cross due to personal failure. This was because the relative environment was flawed. When we examine this thoroughly, we see that in any era, the fulfillment of responsibility in the providence of restoration is not solely a matter of the individual (the responsible party) but rather that relative factors are crucial in determining significant matters.

So, when we consider these relative factors, what can we conclude? It boils down to the issues of people and material. In essence, the environment that separates people and material is what we face. Through the tangled stories here, we live our lives and pursue the purpose of life. Therefore, the objective factors are people and material. For this reason, in the process of restoration, we cannot ignore this, and without securing the absolute condition that the person responsible for that providence is always united with it, we cannot fulfill the mission.

This is why there were the Old Testament and the New Testament in God's providence of restoration. The Old Testament was the time of offering material as sacrifices, while the New Testament was the time of offering a beloved son, a person, as a sacrifice. This is why Christianity has shed much blood. This is an undeniable fact. From this perspective, you must understand how significant the relative environment and conditions are in the providence of restoration.

Furthermore, the issue of how to move these relative conditions and align them before oneself becomes an important matter in the providence of restoration.

Why is that? Because the path of restoration is aimed at fulfilling God's ideals. Why do we fulfill ideals? It is to bring joy to God. How can we bring joy to God? It cannot be done alone. If one is alone, one cannot be joyful. The God who created heaven and earth did not create humanity out of a lack of anything. God created humanity to experience joy. However, to be joyful, there must be a place where hearts and bodies can connect and unite.

The most important issue is the heart's alignment with the other. The place where hearts and bodies can unite is not centered on oneself but must be achieved in a relative relationship. Only then can there be joy. Therefore, if God is alone, He is merely a lonely being. In that state, there are no ideals, no joy, and no happiness. Ultimately, the creation of humanity was for the purpose of fulfilling relationships, so that when I am happy, the other is happy, and when I am sad, the other can also feel sadness.

For this reason, the fulfillment of God's ideal of creation is not something God does alone; it must be achieved through the other. Only through the other can God find joy.

Then, what kind of heart did God have until that relative being was fulfilled? Did He simply feel good all the time? The God who knows that relative conditions determine all subjective content would not have just felt good after creating Adam and Eve. The period until those relative conditions are fulfilled is a time when God earnestly hopes for fulfillment. The greater the love that He earnestly desires, the stronger His inner longing for it to be realized. It is not a matter of leaving things as they are and expecting them to turn out that way; if there is a heart that earnestly longs for fulfillment, then that longing for the other must be the most profound.

If Adam and Eve had been able to perceive God's inner feelings, they would not have been able to fall. That inner feeling refers to the love of a parent for their child. The children did not understand the depth of that parental love. They were unable to reach that understanding. Ultimately, what led to the fall was not the immaturity of age but the immaturity of heart. If they had felt, "That being exists for me. That being is with me. That being is one with me. That being can never be separated from me. That being is involved in every issue of oneness with me," they would not have fallen. Ultimately, the fall occurred because they lacked a point of heart alignment; because their desires diverged from God's will, and because they did not realize how significant their actions were in relation to God's thoughts, they fell. It was due to the lack of a point of heart alignment.

So, what becomes the issue here? When we consider that relative environments and conditions brought about all factors of the fall, we must recognize that the factors of failure are also determined from a relative standpoint. The important question remains: how do we teach that relative being to stay at the point of heart alignment with us? The critical issue in the fall is the relative factors, so how can we restore the fallen humanity to those relative factors? How can we help the other understand our hearts?

When we consider the issue of Cain and Abel, the question becomes how Abel can convey the feelings of joy to Cain so that they can unite. It is not just Abel who should feel good; if Cain had stood in a position where he could feel that goodness, he too could have shared in that joy. However, because they stood in a position where their hearts did not align, the problem arose.

This is true in every era. It was the same for Noah and his son, Abraham and the offering, and also in Jacob's life journey, as well as in the lives of Moses, John the Baptist, and Jesus. Ultimately, the question of how relative beings can achieve heart alignment becomes the most important issue.

How do we find the point of heart alignment between the subject and the object? For example, when we look at Jesus and his three disciples, at the final moment when it was a question of whether he would leave them as the last hope on earth or lose them, if Jesus' heart and the hearts of the disciples had aligned, they would have been able to stand in a position to help Jesus on his path. However, because their emotional directions diverged, the differences in their emotional positions brought about tragic results. This was also true in the relationship between Israel and Jesus, as well as between Judaism and Jesus. Therefore, we must recognize that the question of how to find the point of heart alignment between the subject and the object remains an important matter in the providence of restoration.

If a parent is grieving and shedding tears, and if there is a child laughing beside them, that is disobedience. Why is it disobedience? Because they have fallen into a position where they cannot become one forever. However, when parents are grieving, and the children naturally feel sorrow as well, that is walking the same path. The success of the parents is the success of the children, and the sorrow of the parents manifests as the sorrow of the children. When they walk together, they can occupy the same position in the outcome. This is beyond question.

Then, how can this be made possible? This becomes an important issue. To convey my heart to the heart of the other, it is absolutely impossible to think of oneself. It is absolutely impossible to think of oneself centered on oneself. Why is that? Because it is akin to standing in a position that does not create. Thinking of oneself means standing in a place where there is no relative object, acknowledging that there is no object, and being in a position where one cannot create an environment to fulfill the purpose. In that place, absolute heart alignment cannot occur. Heart alignment is something that cannot even be conceived of.

For this reason, God, who is promoting the will of the providence of restoration, has mobilized numerous religions and presented teachings that say, "Do not think only of yourself, do not elevate yourself, do not be arrogant, be humble and sacrificial." Why has He presented such teachings? Because if one thinks of oneself, one will disregard the environment. That is, standing in a position that denies the other, which is why the culmination of all grievances arises here. Because it arises from relative conditions, one cannot restore it with just oneself. Since the absolute factor is the other, one cannot promote the providence of restoration from a position that thinks centered on oneself. This is akin to standing in a position that does not create; because one stands in a place without a relative being, one becomes a place that does not recognize the need for the other, and in that position, all relative conditions necessary to fulfill the ideal of creation are completely dissolved.

Knowing this, God has been carrying out the providence of restoration through the history of re-creation. Therefore, to stand in God's position, one must create as God did. Creation is self-consumption. In creation, one does not give up. By walking the path of the providence of restoration, what ultimately emerges is the most significant point of heart alignment. This is not a flat plane but a high place like a mountain; when one becomes one centered on that high place, the most profound happiness emerges.

However, to manage that environment, one must go through the process of re-creation, so thinking of oneself is absolutely not the way.

Message of the Sixth God’s Day  
Today, as you know, is the sixth God’s Day. It has been five years in terms of lunar years. The fact that such a God’s Day has been established is unprecedented in history.  
What is God’s Day?  
Until today, in this fallen world, there has been no day to celebrate God. While there have been many days commemorating nations and people centered around themselves, there has been no day commemorating God.  
Looking back at the history leading up to the emergence of God’s Day, it can be said that only after celebrating a victorious day that elevates a good day to the highest standard could we welcome God’s Day among many days.

Good and Bad

I have met you in the midst of busyness.
