You must be sure that God exists.

You have come here to walk a different path from the world. You are different from your own parents and siblings, and even if you were very close friends, once you come here, you cannot be close. Why is that? It is because the standards of good and evil that we pursue are different.

When we say that God exists, it depends on how far we are from that God. Even if you are studying in the same school, there are differences, and even if you receive a salary in the same workplace, there are differences, and that is determined by how close you are to the center and how far you are from it. Ultimately, you can see that it varies according to distance.

Depending on whether the central person in your workplace is good or bad, if you see that person positively, you will get closer to their good side, and if you see them negatively, you will also become bad. The center is merely a standard for judgment. Therefore, if that central being is good, everything becomes a good standard, and if it is bad, everything becomes a bad standard, and that cannot be denied. Here, we are learning about God and Satan, and Satan must be the center representing evil, while God must be the center representing good.

Then, when there are these two centers, there can be no final line connecting those connected to the center. In fact, if such beings exist, it is inevitable that humanity living on this earth belongs to a certain realm. So where is that final line? That is the problem. If you are sure that there are bad and good centers, you cannot help but have an urgent heart to determine the final line.

Can you confidently answer that you know there is a God and that there is evil? Can you be sure that God exists? If you knew God one hundred percent, you wouldn’t need education or anything else. You wouldn’t even need the Teacher.

If God exists and reveals light, it would be the brightest. Even if you are told not to go, you would seek that light. If a person in the light is good, there would be nothing better, and once you cling to it, it becomes eternal and unchanging. Thus, we can conclude that God is unique.

In God's love, there is equality, peace, happiness, and freedom.

So what must we humans have? We must have the most precious love, eternal and unchanging love. If we have that, everything will be resolved. That is why we cannot help but seek that path.

Is there anyone who wishes for change where true love exists? For whom is that love? Christians also call God Father, and if there is something most precious, would they want to become the Father’s possession or their own possession? Can they wish to exist only in God's love?

God's absolute love is better the more you receive it. Where there is love, there is high pressure, and where there is no love, there is low pressure; thus, high and low pressures are exchanged. That is why church movements arise.

True equality cannot exist without love. Happiness and freedom are the same; without love, they cannot exist. Equality and peace must exist for freedom to exist. Even in the desire to be free in the world, one cannot do it alone; one must find freedom centered on someone, in the subject-object relationship. However, even if the subject and object boast of their freedom and dance, when they move in the realm of evil, it cannot be freedom and happiness. That is a freedom that leads to ruin and destruction.

Within the absolute authority that can guarantee freedom, there is peaceful and happy freedom, and where it cannot be guaranteed, there is no freedom. For example, when there are loving parents and loving siblings, in a recognized position, they can block all invasions from the environment, leading to eternal freedom, but in an environment surrounded by enemies, freedom cannot be guaranteed. Ultimately, freedom is a matter of environment.

Especially today, young people must remember that the environment is important for enjoying freedom. In places where one cannot create conditions to protect oneself and guarantee oneself, freedom becomes a kind of indulgence and destruction. In other words, love is eternal and ideal, and centered on that love...
The freedom that is achieved through love can be concluded to be an eternal and unchanging freedom.  
We have come to know that God is the only subject who is eternal and unchanging. Only in Him are there true equality, peace, happiness, and eternal freedom. In a world without love, no peace or freedom can be guaranteed. This is because the very essence of the mind changes.  
So what is Satan? Satan is that which is the complete opposite of God; it is not eternal and is ever-changing, lacking a singular purpose. However, once we understand the fundamental principle of love, we can love both God's people and Satan's people completely together.  
In an evil world, love cannot be found; it is not about caring for one another but rather about dictatorship, centered on oneself. This is why everyone dislikes dictatorship. However, among dictatorships, there is nothing wrong with a dictatorship that loves others more than itself, especially if it is in a position to give everything for others. In such a case, there is God's love present.  
Evil love is a dictatorship that is centered on oneself without considering the other. Freedom that is centered on oneself is evil. Freedom that is centered on others can be allowed in abundance. The world of Satan is finite, changing, and continually shifts its center because it lacks love.

The Posture of a Leader in Front of an Audience  
However, you must first consider that being a leader and a person in charge is not a simple matter. Whether there are a hundred people or a thousand, the larger the environment, the more individuals will each have their own perspective on the speaker, who stands on the platform. You must adopt different attitudes based on whether you are tall or short. The same goes for whether you are fat or thin. If a thin person stands arrogantly, that is not acceptable. You must study how to adapt accordingly. The taller or larger a person is, the more they must adjust their attitude accordingly. You must also consider whether you are Western or Eastern. Depending on whether you have black or blonde hair, you must think about how to establish a standard for the audience and what kind of attitude to adopt when stepping onto the platform.

It deals with the fundamental issues of the universe, which have been divided into materialism and idealism, and it seeks to find solutions to these fundamental philosophical problems and systematize them. Unification ideology is newly established and organized with the purpose of integrating everything and presenting a new worldview and a new perspective on life. 

Therefore, you cannot avoid studying. We will translate these and spread them throughout all universities in America. Then, all the intelligent students in those universities will study them. Therefore, it will be difficult for you to be less skilled than those who will study them in the future. 

As you know, I visited the Army Academy the other day. The reason is that it is close to us and is where the best talents in America gather.
In the future, we are thinking about how to defeat them ideologically. We are currently planning that operation and intend to act on it soon. Once that is accomplished, the CIA and the entire United States will be involved. That is why we are planning this, and in the west, we are currently planning at Stanford University. This university is quite outstanding both internally and externally in the U.S., and many people admire it. If these two institutions start moving, we believe that all scholars in American universities can be united in one action.

Now, as members of the Unification Church, it is obvious that without knowing these three items, one cannot become a global leader or a national leader. You need to understand this. What the trainees here need to know is that we are planning an operation regarding West Point during this training period. We are going to conduct the West Point operation. And in New York City, I will directly lead you in evangelism. So yesterday, I took Kamiya and another person to give special instructions about the activities.

Using vans for evangelism activities
We will park a car at a corner in the busy area of New York and ensure that ten people are in each team, arriving at the destination exactly 30 minutes early, parking the van, and bringing one person at a time to the main lecture hall. We plan to start this activity from this evening. There is no need for lectures now. We will confront them directly. “Is this what young people are doing in a time when America is on the brink of life or death? What is a theater?” We are thinking of bringing young people out like this. It won't take even 30 minutes. Within 20 minutes, we can grab ten people one by one. If we have seven vans, we can bring 70 people at once. We need to carry out such movements.

We need to quickly secure vans. We should instruct to bring two vans today. Once we start this kind of activity, results will follow. There are currently two large buses here, and if you go out to work directly and if there are 40 people on one bus, we need to fill 80 people in two buses. The goal is to bring 80 people to the New York center at a specific time. And those who come to listen to the lectures should be taken back home by the van if possible. By doing this, they will become friendly and may meet personally. Those who brought them can ride together and talk to become closer, and we need to increase the number of members in New York several times within a short period. The issue is how to create over 500 members by autumn.

So what will we do? When autumn comes, I will have to give a major lecture. We need to secure a venue, either at the New York center or the opera house, and declare war on America. Therefore, we need people. This will create issues. Time is running out. The question is how to create a mobilization team of 8,000 members in New York by next year at the latest. We must not fail to do this.

Therefore, I plan to directly engage in activities in Washington. After that, nationwide, all mobilization teams will be equipped with vans to support such activities. We will not be going alone. We will set up in the busiest areas and catch people as they come and go. “Young people cannot continue like this. If you truly love America, follow us. The only way to save America is through this path. The way to eliminate this decadent ideology is through a new ideology.” If we promote this, we can attract all young people at once. The mobilization teams must engage in such activities. That is the plan. If we promote it and no one comes, what is the reason? If we can't do it, I will coach directly. When I say, “Let’s go,” it will happen; it’s just that we haven’t done it.

So we must unite. We must truly engage in a charge operation and lay a foundation within two years. We must discard the past mindset. We need to completely remove the mindset learned during the era of past missionaries. We must pledge to start a new religion that has never existed in history, and you must go out with that conviction. If it doesn’t work this year, will you do it next year? If not next year, will you do it the year after? That’s not how it works. The restoration providence must be done at the right time. If we don’t do it during that period, problems will arise.

We need to unify the principle lectures globally through tapes.
From now on, what the New York church does will become a model for the entire nation. Therefore, we will start from today. I gave special instructions last night. What those special instructions entail is that we must unify the principle lectures globally. In the future, the creation principle should be able to be lectured for 30 minutes, then one and a half hours, two and a half hours, four hours, six hours, and nine hours, creating six stages of time divisions for cassette tapes. Then, the lecture on the fall should be made into 40-minute, one and a half hour, two and a half hour, and four-hour versions, and the restoration principle should also be created in that manner. We need to quickly distribute those recorded tapes to various centers across the nation.

Since we can conduct activities for eight hours in New York, we need to create three lecture rooms. We should prepare several recordings for the creation principle room, the fall principle room, and the restoration principle room. So whenever someone comes to visit, if they ask for time, if they have an hour and a half, we can give them a one and a half-hour tape; if they have two hours, we can give them a two-hour tape; if they have no time, we can give them a 40-minute tape to listen to. Since there are multiple rooms, everyone can go out and do activities. We can have everyone listen to the tapes alone. Then the person in charge should coach them to listen to more lectures. As a result, there will be more researchers and more members, so we need to promote this activity. Thus, someone who has listened to the 40-minute tape will want to listen to the one-hour tape even if they are told not to, and they will come back to listen again. As they listen to one and a half hours, two and a half hours, they will keep coming back for four hours, six hours… even if they are told not to come, they will automatically come.

Evangelism activities through recorded lectures
Also, each person can prepare a recorder and record themselves. Since the original is made into a booklet and read directly, if they look at the book and record their pronunciation on a cassette, anyone can listen to it, and the lecture will be as if they are giving it themselves. While taking someone along, they can play the recording they made in their own voice, and after about 15 minutes, they can ask if there are any questions. If there are questions, they can answer them, and if not, they can continue listening. By coaching like this, we won’t need famous lecturers. Anyone from the national activity team can become a lecturer and engage in activities, thus preventing a shortage of talent. If that happens, the listeners will think, “Oh, this person is giving a lecture with such skill through the recording tape!” and naturally, they will gain respect and achieve results.

We can also approach shop owners in the city and say, “Instead of just waiting, if you’re bored, why not listen to this?” If they say they don’t have time, we can ask how much time they can spare. If they say 40 minutes, we can suggest they listen to a 40-minute tape. We can say it will be interesting, leave it with them, and come back after 40 minutes for a Q&A. If they don’t have a recorder, we can lend them one, and we can go around the city evangelizing.

Implement this worldwide immediately
Now, Neil Salonen, you need to quickly plan and implement this. We need to start from Washington and do this everywhere. This also needs to be done in Japan and Korea. You should discuss this with President Kim and get the teacher's approval to proceed. The teacher is planning to unify this and develop it into a global activity. Do you understand? Raise your hand if you agree.

Until now, we have said there are no people, but in reality, there are no people. However, with just a few tapes prepared, we can evangelize ten houses or twenty houses even without people. And since they won’t feel bad but will be grateful, we can also receive donations. There is a way to engage in activities without making money. With this, even those who just joined yesterday can record on a tape and share it for evangelism. I see this as the only last path to rapidly create many of our members nationwide in a short time.

From today, or rather since yesterday… we need to contact various countries through the president, including Japan and Korea. We will organize this globally, so we need to send out official documents quickly. The teacher has given special instructions, and the president should draft this in the teacher's name and send it out worldwide. Then, we will evaluate which country implemented it first and which country did well, and we will select the best one to set as a standard for global imitation.

We need to penetrate the academic world using a communist-style approach. Ultimately, we can say, “Don’t you need this material?” and by allowing them to use it, the tape could be treated as a treasure in their household. It’s not about buying books. That’s how it will be. We can also gather people from the neighborhood who are not our members and share it with them all at once. Do you think that will work? “Yes.”

We can also raise funds by selling recorded tapes.
So you need to execute this quickly, quickly. If there are ten thousand recorded tapes, that means ten thousand people can listen to them. We need to record a hundred at once and go out to play them and gather around to listen. Therefore, we need to create a recording room.

To record, we can place a hundred recorders in a quiet room and do it all at once. If we do it in one room, it will all be recorded, right? We are planning to do it in such a room, so please prepare for that.

Then, we should send the tapes immediately to those who send money… this will create competition for sending them. If they just send the price of the recording tape, we will send them all promptly. This is how we will do it for our members worldwide.

Find out how much it costs and quickly send out an official document stating the amount. Do you understand? “Yes.” Send out the official document, stating how much the recorder costs and how many tapes there are, and tell them to send money in order to receive them.

In Japan, we should import several thousand at once. Isn’t there not much tax here? Are you all going to buy tapes? “Yes.” So will our members. As you engage in activities, if members want this, they should order it. If they order, we will sell it at wholesale prices… By selling at wholesale prices, you will also generate funds for your activities. You just need to keep selling.

“It’s not just for members…” (Interpreter) Yes, yes. What is there for the interpreter to keep asking? Just translate as it is. If they want recording tapes, they can get them anytime… “Not just for our members, but for others…” (Interpreter) Yes, it’s good for outsiders or shopkeepers too. (Laughter) We will import recording tapes at wholesale prices and give them to them, allowing you to generate profits and raise funds.

You should evangelize by recording in your own voice.
And because it is recorded in your own voice, people will be amazed, thinking, “This person seems small and insignificant, but they are a lecturer.” If you play your voice in your area and promote it, there will be no need to invite them. Those who have heard it will come and say, “Please give me some time.” If you say, “Oh, I don’t have time,” you can say, “I’ll treat you to dinner…” and by doing so, you can lay the foundation to work. Once they listen, they will definitely be curious and say, “Let’s meet.” If you say, “I don’t have time,” you will end up inviting them all to dinner. That is possible. Then, if you gather all the neighbors, they will say they will go. It requires gathering several people to say they will go.

To do this, the challenge is how to create a group of 20 people in a short period. The teacher believes that once we create 20 people, it will gradually grow from there. We need to devise such plans and create mobilization teams… But you are unaware of this. Do you think evangelism is difficult? It’s easy, right? “Yes.” So from now on, think that America is moving.

From today, since missionaries have entered various cultural centers in America, if a college graduate comes into our church, there will be no need for years of training. If we send them out after just a month of training, they will want to go as missionaries to their own countries. Then we will send them. Now, they can go within a month of entering, and even if they entered yesterday, they can go today. This means we are rapidly expanding into the world, and that is the teacher’s perspective. You need to understand this and establish such traditions based on principles.

Because we have established global achievements and traditions, from now on, Mr. Moon and the Unification Church will become famous. It’s not just about U.S. senators. (The following remarks are not recorded) *
